<a id="10408" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#9516" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="10415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10415" class="Bound">Σ</a> <a id="10417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10417" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="10420" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10421" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10421" class="Bound">⊢L</a> <a id="10424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1980" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="10426" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10426" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="10428" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="10434" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="10437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#9516" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="10444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10415" class="Bound">Σ</a> <a id="10446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10417" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="10449" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10421" class="Bound">⊢L</a> <a id="10452" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1980" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="10454" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#9516" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="10461" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10415" class="Bound">Σ</a> <a id="10463" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10417" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="10466" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10426" class="Bound">⊢M</a>

<a id="10470" class="Comment">{-
⊢subst : ∀ {Γ Δ xs ys ρ}
  → (∀ {x}   → x ∈ xs       →  free (ρ x) ⊆ ys)
  → (∀ {x A} → x ∈ xs       →  Γ ∋ x ⦂ A  →  Δ ⊢ ρ x ⦂ A)
    --------------------------------------------------------------
  → (∀ {M A} → free M ⊆ xs  →  Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A  →  Δ ⊢ subst ys ρ M ⦂ A)
⊢subst Σ ⊢ρ ⊆xs (` ⊢x)
    =  ⊢ρ (⊆xs here) ⊢x
⊢subst {Γ} {Δ} {xs} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ ⊆xs (`λ_ {x = x} {A = A} {N = N} ⊢N)
    = `λ_ {x = y} {A = A} (⊢subst {Γ′} {Δ′} {xs′} {ys′} {ρ′} Σ′ ⊢ρ′ ⊆xs′ ⊢N)
  where
  y   =  fresh ys
  Γ′  =  Γ , x ⦂ A
  Δ′  =  Δ , y ⦂ A
  xs′ =  x ∷ xs
  ys′ =  y ∷ ys
  ρ′  =  ρ , x ↦ ` y

  Σ′ : ∀ {w} → w ∈ xs′ →  free (ρ′ w) ⊆ ys′
  Σ′ {w} w∈′ with w ≟ x
  ...            | yes refl    =  ⊆-++₁
  ...            | no  w≢      =  ⊆-++₂ ∘ Σ (there⁻¹ w∈′ w≢)
  
  ⊆xs′ :  free N ⊆ xs′
  ⊆xs′ =  \\-to-∷ ⊆xs

  ⊢σ : ∀ {w C} → w ∈ ys → Δ ∋ w ⦂ C → Δ′ ∋ w ⦂ C
  ⊢σ w∈ ⊢w  =  S (fresh-lemma w∈) ⊢w

  ⊢ρ′ : ∀ {w C} → w ∈ xs′ → Γ′ ∋ w ⦂ C → Δ′ ⊢ ρ′ w ⦂ C
  ⊢ρ′ {w} _ Z with w ≟ x
  ...         | yes _             =  ` Z
  ...         | no  w≢            =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ⊢ρ′ {w} w∈′ (S w≢ ⊢w) with w ≟ x
  ...         | yes refl          =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ...         | no  _             =  ⊢rename {Δ} {Δ′} {ys} ⊢σ (Σ w∈) (⊢ρ w∈ ⊢w)
              where
              w∈  =  there⁻¹ w∈′ w≢

⊢subst Σ ⊢ρ ⊆xs (⊢L · ⊢M)
    =  ⊢subst Σ ⊢ρ L⊆ ⊢L · ⊢subst Σ ⊢ρ M⊆ ⊢M
  where
  L⊆ = trans-⊆ ⊆-++₁ ⊆xs
  M⊆ = trans-⊆ ⊆-++₂ ⊆xs
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

    <a id="12462" class="Comment">---------------</a>
  <a id="12480" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12482" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12412" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="12484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1752" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12417" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12488" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1752" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="12490" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12419" class="Bound">A</a>

  <a id="12543" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12545" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#7057" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="12549" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12528" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="12551" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Collections.md %}{% raw %}#1828" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="12553" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#4424" class="Function">free</a> <a id="12558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12538" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12560" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.List.Base.html#1336" class="Function Operator">++</a> <a id="12563" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#4424" class="Function">free</a> <a id="12569" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12534" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="12571" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Collections.md %}{% raw %}#1901" class="Function Operator">\\</a> <a id="12574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12530" class="Bound">x</a><a id="12575" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12579" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12528" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="12583" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1411" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12530" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1411" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⦂</a> <a id="12589" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12532" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1752" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12534" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="12595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1752" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="12597" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12536" class="Bound">B</a>

    <a id="12617" class="Comment">---------------------</a>
  <a id="12641" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12528" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="12645" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1752" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12534" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="12649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#5404" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="12651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12530" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#5404" class="Function Operator">:=</a> <a id="12656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12538" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#5404" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="12660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1752" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="12662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12536" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="12664" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12508" class="Function">⊢substitution₀</a> <a id="12679" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12681" class="Symbol">{!!}</a>

<a id="12687" class="Comment">{-
⊢substitution : ∀ {Γ x A N B M}
  → Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ⦂ B
  → Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A
    --------------------
  → Γ ⊢ N [ x := M ] ⦂ B
⊢substitution {Γ} {x} {A} {N} {B} {M} ⊢N ⊢M =
  ⊢weaker {Γ} {ys} ⊆N[x:=M]
    (⊢substitution₀
      (refl-⊆ (//-lemma {Γ} {ys}))
      (⊢stronger {Γ , x ⦂ A} {x ∷ ys} ⊆N ⊢N)
      (⊢stronger {Γ} {ys} ⊆M ⊢M))
    where
    ys = free M ++ (free N \\ x)
    ⊆N : free N ⊆ x ∷ ys
    ⊆N = ?
    ⊆M : free M ⊆ ys
    ⊆M = ?
    ⊆N[x:=M] : free (N [ x := M ]) ⊆ ys
    ⊆N[x:=M] = ?
-}</a>
  
<a id="13190" class="Comment">{-
⊢substitution : ∀ {Γ x A N B M} →
  Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ⦂ B →
  Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A →
  --------------------
  Γ ⊢ N [ x := M ] ⦂ B
⊢substitution {Γ} {x} {A} {N} {B} {M} ⊢N ⊢M =
  subst {Γ′ , x ⦂ A} {Γ′} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ ⊢N′
  where
  ys   =  free M ++ (free N \\ x)
  Δ    =  Γ // ys
  ⊢N′  =  rename {Γ , x ⦂ A} {Δ , x ⦂ A} ? ⊢N
  ⊢M′  =  rename {Γ} {Δ} ? ⊢M
  
  -- rename is no longer sufficiently powerful
  -- it can do weakening but not strengthening

  -- not clear where and how def&#39;n of ys gets used

  ⊢subst {Γ′} {Γ} {xs} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ {N} {B} ⊆xs ⊢N
  where
  Γ′     =  Γ , x ⦂ A
  xs     =  free N
  ρ      =  ∅ , x ↦ M

  Σ : ∀ {w} → w ∈ xs → free (ρ w) ⊆ ys
  Σ {w} w∈ y∈ with w ≟ x
  ...            | yes _                   =  ⊆-++₁ y∈
  ...            | no w≢ rewrite ∈-[_] y∈  =  ⊆-++₂ (∈-≢-to-\\ w∈ w≢)
  
  ⊢ρ : ∀ {w B} → w ∈ xs → Γ′ ∋ w ⦂ B → Γ ⊢ ρ w ⦂ B
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ Z         with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes _     =  ⊢M
  ...                    | no  w≢    =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ (S w≢ ⊢w) with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes refl  =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ...                    | no  _     =  ` ⊢w

  ⊆xs : free N ⊆ xs
  ⊆xs x∈ = x∈
-}</a>

<a id="14359" class="Comment">{-
⊢substitution : ∀ {Γ x A N B M} →
  Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ⦂ B →
  Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A →
  --------------------
  Γ ⊢ N [ x := M ] ⦂ B
⊢substitution {Γ} {x} {A} {N} {B} {M} ⊢N ⊢M =
  subst {Γ′ , x ⦂ A} {Γ′} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ ⊢N′
  where
  ys   =  free M ++ (free N \\ x)
  Γ′   =  Γ // ys
  ⊢N′  =  rename {Γ , x ⦂ A} {Γ′ , x ⦂ A} ? ⊢N
  ⊢M′  =  rename {Γ} {Γ′} ? ⊢M
  
  -- rename is no longer sufficiently powerful
  -- it can do weakening but not strengthening

  -- not clear where and how def&#39;n of ys gets used

  ⊢subst {Γ′} {Γ} {xs} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ {N} {B} ⊆xs ⊢N
  where
  Γ′     =  Γ , x ⦂ A
  xs     =  free N
  ρ      =  ∅ , x ↦ M

  Σ : ∀ {w} → w ∈ xs → free (ρ w) ⊆ ys
  Σ {w} w∈ y∈ with w ≟ x
  ...            | yes _                   =  ⊆-++₁ y∈
  ...            | no w≢ rewrite ∈-[_] y∈  =  ⊆-++₂ (∈-≢-to-\\ w∈ w≢)
  
  ⊢ρ : ∀ {w B} → w ∈ xs → Γ′ ∋ w ⦂ B → Γ ⊢ ρ w ⦂ B
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ Z         with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes _     =  ⊢M
  ...                    | no  w≢    =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ (S w≢ ⊢w) with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes refl  =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ...                    | no  _     =  ` ⊢w

  ⊆xs : free N ⊆ xs
  ⊆xs x∈ = x∈
-}</a>

<a id="15530" class="Comment">{-
⊢substitution : ∀ {Γ x A N B M} →
  Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ⦂ B →
  Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A →
  --------------------
  Γ ⊢ N [ x := M ] ⦂ B
⊢substitution {Γ} {x} {A} {N} {B} {M} ⊢N ⊢M =
  ⊢subst {Γ′} {Γ} {xs} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ {N} {B} ⊆xs ⊢N
  where
  Γ′     =  Γ , x ⦂ A
  xs     =  free N
  ys     =  free M ++ (free N \\ x)
  ρ      =  ∅ , x ↦ M

  Σ : ∀ {w} → w ∈ xs → free (ρ w) ⊆ ys
  Σ {w} w∈ y∈ with w ≟ x
  ...            | yes _                   =  ⊆-++₁ y∈
  ...            | no w≢ rewrite ∈-[_] y∈  =  ⊆-++₂ (∈-≢-to-\\ w∈ w≢)
  
  ⊢ρ : ∀ {w B} → w ∈ xs → Γ′ ∋ w ⦂ B → Γ ⊢ ρ w ⦂ B
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ Z         with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes _     =  ⊢M
  ...                    | no  w≢    =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ (S w≢ ⊢w) with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes refl  =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ...                    | no  _     =  ` ⊢w

  ⊆xs : free N ⊆ xs
  ⊆xs x∈ = x∈
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Preservation

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="16447" class="Comment">{-
preservation : ∀ {Γ M N A}
  →  Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A
  →  M ⟶ N
     ---------
  →  Γ ⊢ N ⦂ A
preservation (` ⊢x) ()
preservation (`λ ⊢N) ()
preservation (⊢L · ⊢M) (ξ-⟹₁ L⟶L′)        =  preservation ⊢L L⟶L′ · ⊢M
preservation (⊢V · ⊢M) (ξ-⟹₂ valV M⟶M′)   =  ⊢V · preservation ⊢M M⟶M′
preservation ((`λ ⊢N) · ⊢W) (β-⟹ valW)      =  ⊢substitution ⊢N ⊢W
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
